// HF + 6m band JT65/JT9 callsign+grid square database for JTDX software
// being used by decoders based on the matched filter(button Hint)
// and for filtering out some false FTRSD decodes. 
// Contains 34323 unique callsigns.
//
// It is based on JT65/JT9 spots data made by JTAlert software 
// http://hamapps.com
// and collected from http://hamspots.net resource.  
//
// This file shall be put in the log directory (File->Open log directory) 
// to get maximum decoding efficiency from JTDX software. 
//
// Created by Igor UA3DJY on June 12th, 2017, using raw data collected
// between November 1st 2016 and June 12th 2017, Python script 
// made by Arvo ES1JA and Perl scripts for data processing,
// with grateful acknowledgement to Laurie VK3AMA for the contribution.
//
// This file is not compatible with JTDX software versions 
// earlier than v17.6
//
